inspector it shall be his duty to inspect all buildings and premises in the city and he shall see that all buildings and premises are kept free from empty boxes waste paper ashes and all other material or rubbish which may be liable to cause or spread fire and for the purpose of remedying any condition that may in his opinion be liable to cause or spread fire and he shall enforce the ordinances of the city relating to the prevention of fires b for the purpose of making such inspections the chief of the fire department is hereby empowered to appoint one or more deputy inspectors who when appointed shall have all the powers and duties herein prescribed for the chief of the fire department as fire inspector c the members of the fire department appointed as inspectors shall file with the chief of the fire department a daily report in detail of the work done premises inspected and the condition of the same which report shall be kept in the permanent files by the chief of the fire department for inspection by the city administrator mayor or council 4   923 fire chief  duties and powers a the chief of the fire department shall be the commanding officer of the department under the supervision of the city administrator and shall be responsible to the city administrator for its proper management the property of the department shall be in his care and for its safety and proper assignment he shall be directly responsible to the city administrator b it shall be the duty of the chief to see that all rules regulations and orders prescribed by the city council or city administrator are promptly and faithfully respected and obeyed and whenever any violation of the same is reported to him or comes under his personal observation he shall promptly investigate the same and report the matter to the city administrator c the chief shall respond to all alarms and shall upon arrival at the scene of the fire at once assume command taking every precaution for the protection of life and property he shall make a monthly report of the number of men on duty and of the condition of the several stations and property belonging to the department he shall visit each department house in the service as often as practicable and see that the quarters are in good order and well cared for he shall not absent himself from the city without the consent of the city administrator and when leave of absence is granted he shall immediately notify his assistant chief it shall be his duty to examine into or cause to be examined into by the assistant chief or other subordinates the cause origin and circumstances of all fires occurring within the city he shall have authority at all times day or night in the performance of the duties imposed by this chapter to enter upon and examine any building or premises where a fire has occurred and other buildings or premises adjoining or near the same he shall make a report to the city administrator in writing as soon after the occurrence of any fire as possible giving the time date and location of the fire the owner or lessee of the property amount of loss amount of insurance and stating the result of the investigation as to the cause origin and circumstances of such fire    91 drinking or profane language prohibited at fire station no drinking or profane language shall be indulged at the fire station commissioner 4   943 secs 12331252  reserved article iii  open burning prohibited open burning  exceptions open burning is prohibited except as provided below 1 open burning of leaves tree branches or yard trimmings originating on the premises of private residences and burned on those premises 2 open burning in connection with the preparation of food for immediate consumption 3 campfires and fires used solely for recreational purposes ceremonial occasions or human warmth fire set for the purpose of human warmth must use only clean wood products woody vegetation leaves or wood which is not coated with stain paint glue or other coating material and not treated lumber 4 fires purposely set in accordance with smoke management guidelines for vegetative debris burning operations in south carolina administered by the state forestry commission and acceptable to the department to include the following a prescribed burning of forest lands for specific management practices b fires purposely set for agricultural control of diseases weeds pests and for other specific agricultural purposes c open burning of trees brush grass and other vegetable matter for game management purposes 5 open burning in areas other than predominately residential for the purpose of land clearing or rightofway maintenance this will be exempt only if the following minimum conditions are followed a the location of the burning must be a sufficient distance but not less than 1000 feet from public roadways and all residential commercial and industrial sites not a part of the contiguous property on which the burning is conducted b winds during the time of the burning must be away from any area in which the ambient air may be significantly affected by smoke from the burning if that area contains a public roadway or a residential commercial or industrial site c the material to be burned must have been generated onsite and not moved to the site from another location d the amount of dirt on the material being burned must be minimized e no heavy oils asphaltic materials items containing natural or synthetic rubber or any materials other than plant growth may be burned f the initial burning must be started only between the hours of  am and  pm  no combustible material may be added to the fire between  pm of one day and  am the following day g no more than two piles of 30 feet by 30 feet or equivalent may be burned within a sixacre area at one time h in the case of land cleaning all salvageable timber and pulpwood must be removed 6 fires set for the purposes of training firefighting personnel and conducted at permanent firefighter training facilities prior department approval is required in order to obtain the exemption as a permanently established training site fires set for the purpose of firefighter training at nonpermanent locations must receive department approval prior to the initiation of any burning activity materials used for firefighter training cannot contain asbestos heavy oils asphaltic material plastic or rubber without express written consent from the department 7 open burning on the property where it occurs of residential construction waste from building and construction operations will be exempt only if the following conditions are met a the material being burned is residential construction waste associated with the building and construction of one and twofamily dwellings only b the location of the burning is at least 500 feet from any occupied structure other than a dwelling or structure located on the property on which the burning is conducted c heavy oils treated wood products asphaltic materials items containing natural or synthetic rubber or any other trade wastes which produce smoke in excess of 40 percent opacity are not burned d the burning does not occur during the ozone season april 1  e the burning is conducted only between the hours of  am and  pm 8 open burning in remote or specified areas a for nonrecurring unusual circumstances b for experimental burning for purposes of data gathering and research however prior approval for these types of burning in subsection 8 of this section must be obtained from the department i 9142010 general regulations a a written report or warning to a person of a violation at one site shall be considered adequate notice of the regulation and subsequent observed violations at the same or different site will result in appropriate legal action b open burning may be conducted in certain situations if no undesirable levels are or will be created the authority to conduct open burning under this regulation does not exempt or excuse the person responsible for the burning from the consequences of or the damages or injuries resulting from the burning and does not exempt or excuse anyone from complying with other applicable laws and with ordinances regulations and orders of governmental entities having jurisdiction even though the burning is otherwise conducted in compliance with this regulation c the department reserves the right to impose other or different restrictions and exemptions on open burning in addition to those enumerate above whenever in the judgment of the department such is necessary to realize the purpose of this regulation ii 9142010 penalties any person violating any provision of this article shall be deemed guilty of an offense and shall be subject to a fine up to $50000 or imprisonment of not more than 30 days or both upon conviction each day of violation shall be considered a separate offense  permits a permit is hereby required for any burning allowed under this article and must be obtained from the city code enforcement officer who shall promptly notify the fire chief of the issuance of any permit the city code public health nuisances definition of public health nuisances any act of any person or corporation whereby the health or life of any individual may be endangered injured or impaired or which causes any disease is hereby declared a nuisance it shall be unlawful for any owner occupant or agent of lots or premises whether occupied or vacant within the city limits to permit such property to become unsanitary by allowing any offensive matter or thing upon such lot or premises which may be detrimental to health or to permit any trash rubbish waste refuse manure straw hay or thing to accumulate and remain upon such premises or to throw deposit or cause to be thrown or deposited upon any vacant lot or premises such thing which may endanger injure or damage anothers health or property 1   1130 abatement of public nuisances it shall be lawful for the city council to declare as nuisances things the existence of which may be deemed unhealthy or harmful to the citizens of the city and such nuisances may be abated by the code enforcement officer pursuant to directions from the board at the property owners expense and upon said owners failure to abate the municipal authorities shall remove such nuisance at the expense of the person who shall have caused or allowed the same from any occupant or tenant or premises or in the case it affects the freehold from the owner who after of a misdemeanor 3   1132 secs 14221445  reserved article iii  prevention of mosquito breeding unlawful collection of standing or flowing water it shall be unlawful to have keep maintain cause or permit within the limits of the city any collection of standing or flowing water in which mosquitoes breed or are likely to breed unless such collection of water is treated so as to effectually prevent such breeding 1   1140 definitions the following words terms and phrases when used in this article shall have the meanings ascribed to them in this section except where the context clearly indicates a different meaning collections of water means to be those contained in ditches pools ponds excavations holes depressions open cesspools privy vaults fountains cisterns tanks shallow wells barrels troughs except horse troughs in frequent use urns cans boxes bottles tubs buckets defective house roof gutters tanks of flush closets or other similar water containers 2   1141 approved methods of treating water collections the methods of treatment of any collection of water directed toward the prevention of breeding mosquitoes shall be approved by the accredited code enforcement officer and may be any one or more of the following 1 screening with wire netting of at least 16 meshes to the inch each way or with any other material that will effectually prevent the ingress or egress of mosquitoes 2 complete emptying every seven days of unscreened containers together with their thorough drying and cleaning 3 using a larvacide approved and applied under the direction of the code enforcement officer 4 cleaning and keeping sufficiently free of vegetable growth and other obstructions and stocking with mosquitodestroying fish 5 filling or draining to the satisfaction of the code enforcement officer his agent or accredited representative 6 proper disposal by removal or destruction of tin cans tin boxes or empty or broken bottles and similar articles likely to hold water 3   1142 evidence of mosquito breeding the natural presence of mosquito larvae in standing or running water shall be prima facie evidence that mosquitoes are breeding there and failure to prevent such breeding within three days after notice by the code enforcement officer his authorized agent or representative shall be deemed a violation of this section 4   1143 abatement conditions should the person or persons firm or corporation responsible for conditions giving rise to the breeding of mosquitoes fail or refuse to take necessary measures to prevent the same within three days after due notice has been given to them the code enforcement officer or his authorized agent is hereby authorized to do so and all necessary costs incurred by him for this purpose shall be charged against the property owner or other person firm or corporation offending as the case may be 5   1144 right of entry for the purpose of enforcing the provisions of this article the code enforcement officer or his city  and if conditions specified in this chapter are found to exist the code enforcement officer or the city administrator may declare such conditions to constitute a public nuisance  10102017 notification of property owner of public nuisance upon any determination that conditions constituting a public nuisance exist on a property pursuant to this chapter the code enforcement officer shall notify the owner thereof in the following manner 1 the code enforcement officer shall serve upon such property owner a written notice of the declaration of a public nuisance that must a include a description of the real property sufficient to identify the property  b include a statement of the violation or violations that constitute a public nuisance along with why the notice is being issued  c include a description of the corrective action that the property owner must take to remediate the violation and a deadline which shall not be less than 20 days from the date of service of such notice by which the property owner must take such remedial action  d inform the property owner of the right to appeal the determination that conditions on such property constitute a public nuisance  and e include a statement that if the conditions on the property are not remediated within the established time period the city shall enter onto the property to remediate such conditions and assess the citys costs therefor upon the property owner that may be collected in the same manner that city taxes may be collected including placing a lien upon the property in the amount of the citys costs foreclosing upon the property and selling the property at a tax sale 2 the notice discussed above shall be served in the following manner a in the event that the property records for such property indicate that the property owner resides within the city the code enforcement officer shall make every effort to personally serve the notice upon the property owner provided the property owner shall sign a certificate of receipt of such notice and discuss the ways in which the property owner may remediate the conditions on the property  or b in the event that the property records for such property indicate that the property owner resides outside of the city or the code enforcement officer has been unable to meet with property owner the code enforcement officer shall serve the notice upon the property owner by certified mail at the last known address thereof  or c in the event that the notice is returned as undeliverable a copy thereof shall be posted in a conspicuous place on or about the property and upon such posting service shall be deemed complete  10102017 failure of property owner to remediate nuisance conditions  recovery of costs if the property owner fails to remediate the conditions on the property constituting a public nuisance in the manner and within the time set forth in the notice provided for in section 14110 the city staff or a private contractor employed by the city may thereafter enter onto the property to take such action noted on the notice to remediate the conditions constituting the nuisance the city staff or the private contractor shall keep an accurate account of the actual cost of such remediation which shall be forwarded to the citys financial director the citys costs incurred pursuant to this section including any legal related thereto shall become a lien upon the real estate upon which the condition constituting a nuisance existed that is collectable in the same manner as municipal taxes including foreclosure and the sale of the property at a tax sale  10102017 right of appeal  appellate process a the owner of any property which is the subject of a nuisance declaration made pursuant to this chapter or any notice issued pursuant to this chapter shall have the right to appeal such determination to the city council provided that a written application for appeal is filed with the clerk to the city council no later than 20 days after the day the notice provided for in this chapter was served the filing of an appeal shall stay any action by the city to remediate conditions constituting a nuisance upon the property until such time as the appeal may be decided upon by the city council b any appeal subject to this chapter shall be conducted using the following procedure 1 all hearings related to any such appeal shall be in an open session of the city council wherein a quorum is present the city administrator and the codes enforcement officer shall first present the case to the city council and the property owner or a representative of the property owner which may be an attorney shall respond 2 any such hearing shall be recorded and copies thereof made available to the property owner at no charge upon request 3 hearings shall not be subject to the rules of evidence but the mayor of the city council or some other presiding officer or city council may mandate at the discretion of the presiding officer that only relevant information be presented 4 the city council may uphold or overturn the determination of the city administrator or code enforcement officer by majority vote taken in open session the city council may decide upon any such appeal at the initial hearing or may take the matter under consideration to be decided upon in open session of the city council at a later date the city council shall provide as part of any motion deciding the matter any factual findings upon which the decision is based 5 a property owner shall have the right to apply to the appropriate court for a writ of certiorari to correct errors of law related to the decision of the city council application for review shall be made in the manner required by law within 30 days of the hearing before city council on such matter if the decision is then made or service upon the property owner of the decision of the city council if made at a later date  10102017 offenses and miscellaneous provisions reserved article ix  fireworks and explosives sale storage transportation or use of impermissible fireworks  enumeration of permissible fireworks it shall be unlawful for persons to possess sell offer for sale store transport or use within this city any fireworks other than the permissible fireworks permitted for sale and use under state law 1 exceptions to application of article nothing in this article shall apply to 1 the shipping sale possession and use of fireworks for public displays and such items of fireworks which are to be used for public display only and which are otherwise prohibited for sale and use within the state shall include display shells designed to be fired from mortars and display set pieces of fireworks classified by the regulations of the interstate commerce commission as class b special fireworks and shall not include such items of commercial fireworks as cherry bombs tubular salutes repeating bombs aerial bombs and torpedoes  2 the manufacture storage sale or use of signals necessary for the safe operation of railroads or other public or private transportation  3 illuminating devices for photographic use  4 the military or naval forces of the state or united states  5 peace officers  and 6 the sale or use of blank cartridges for ceremonial theatrical or athletic events 4 permits and other requirements for fireworks displays  penalty for violation a any person who desires to hold a public fireworks display shall first obtain a permit from the mayor and city council in triplicate the manufacturer or wholesaler supplying the fireworks display material shall retain one copy of the permit and the person putting on the display shall retain one copy one copy shall be forwarded to the state fire marshals office b all fireworks display material shall be purchased manufacturer or wholesaler licensed in the state who will supply insurance protection for any accidents that might take place during the display except as otherwise provided for in this article c any display requiring shells to be fired from mortars or set pieces more than 16 feet high shall be classified as type a and when such display is used an experienced fireworks operator shall be in charge for the protection of spectators any display commonly called a local or family display which includes no uncased shells and no shells larger than regular 100 aerial or set pieces larger than ten feet may be fired by persons putting on the display who shall assume responsibility for insurance d no commercial fireworks item such as cherry bombs tnt m80s or other domestic items of commercial fireworks of a similar type shall be considered as display fireworks 6 sales to and purchases from unlicensed persons prohibited  records shall be kept open no wholesaler shall be allowed to sell fireworks to any nonlicensed jobber or retailer and the records of all retailers jobbers and wholesalers shall be open for inspection by authorized officials to check sales or purchases retailers may purchase fireworks only from a manufacturer jobber or wholesaler licensed to do business in the state 8 manner in which fireworks shall be stored by wholesalers fireworks to be sold at wholesale shall be stored in a room set aside for the storage of fireworks only over the entrance to this room shall be posted a sign reading fireworksno smokingkeep open flames away 9 manner in which fireworks shall be stored and displayed by retailers all retailers shall store permissible fireworks in the original unbroken containers in which such fireworks were shipped and received any such fireworks that are displayed or offered in bulk outside such original containers shall be displayed in accordance with rules and regulations promulgated and adopted by the state fire marshal no fireworks shall be displayed in windows or where the sun may shine onto the fireworks at all places where fireworks are stored or sold the area used by the patrons shall be unobstructed with clear access to an outside door such areas where fireworks are stored must have posted signs containing the words fireworks for saleno smoking allowed in letters not less than four inches high no person under the age of 18 years shall be employed as a salesman or handler of fireworks 10 fireworks shall not be kept for sale near certain flammable substances fireworks shall not be sold or kept for sale in a place of business where paint oils varnishes turpentine or gasoline or other flammable substances are kept in unbroken containers unless in a separate and distinct section or department of the store 11 sale of fireworks to minors and discharge of fireworks in certain circumstances unlawful it shall be unlawful to 1 offer for sale or to sell permissible fireworks to of drugs in the workplace a the illegal manufacture distribution dispensation possession or use of narcotics drugs or other controlled substances is strictly prohibited on premises owned leased or controlled by the city b violation of this policy will result in immediate discipline up to and including discharge c employees will be given a copy of this policy and will be required to sign a form acknowledging its receipt by continuing to work the employee agrees that he will abide by the policy as a condition of employment failure to sign the form or abide by the policy will result in discipline up to and including discharge d as a condition of employment employees agree to notify the city within five calendar days after any criminal conviction for the manufacture distribution dispensation possession or use of narcotics drugs or other controlled substances at the workplace criminal conviction means a finding of guilt an imposition of a sentence a plea of no contest or a plea of guilty e the city will notify all federal contracting agencies or grantors of such conviction within ten days after receiving notice of the conviction f law enforcement authorities will be notified whenever illegal drugs are found in the workplace 1   i use of drugs while not at the workplace a the illegal manufacture distribution dispensation possession or use of narcotics drugs or controlled substances either off the premises or on nonwork time or both is prohibited and will result in discipline up to and including discharge b employees must notify the city of any drugrelated convictions within five calendar days after such conviction c the term conviction means a finding of guilt imposition of a sentence a plea of no contest or a plea of guilty 2   ii drug free awareness program a drug abuse in the workplace is dangerous because it leads to physical impairment loss of judgment safety violations and the risk of injury or possible death b in order to prevent these consequences of drug abuse the city has implemented the above policy to ensure that the workplace remains drug free c in lieu of termination for a drugrelated conviction in the workplace the employee may be required to enter into a drug rehabilitation program 3   iii secs 1635516381  reserved article xiv  juvenile curfew prohibitions  exceptions it is unlawful for any minor 16 years of age or younger to loiter wander stroll or play in or upon the public streets highways roads alleys parks playgrounds or other public places vacant lots or any place unsupervised by an adult having the lawful authority to be at such places between the hours of  midnight and  am of any day and provided that the provisions of this section shall not apply in the following instances 1 when a minor is accompanied by his parent legal guardian or other adult person over the age of 21 years having the lawful care and custody of the minor  2 when the minor is upon an emergency errand directed by his parent or legal guardian or other adult person over the age of 21 years having the lawful care and custody of the minor  3 when the minor is returning directly home from a school activity recreational activity or dance  4 when a minor is returning directly home from lawful employment that makes it necessary to be in the above referenced places during the prescribed period of time  5 when the minor is in a motor vehicle with parental consent for normal travel which travel city is excepted in all cases from the curfew 1   violations any minor found in violation of section 16382 shall be subject to the following courtesy summons and the contacting of the parent guardian or other person having custody or control 2   parental responsibilities it shall be unlawful for the parent guardian or other person having custody or control of any child 16 years of age or younger to permit or by insufficient control to allow such child to be in or upon the public streets or any other place within the city between the hours of  midnight and  am on any day except in circumstances set out in section 16382 3   penalties any person found in violation of this article shall be subject to one of the following and each violation of this article shall constitute a separate offense 1 first offense courtesy summons 2 second offense fine not to exceed $10000 at the discretion of the court 3 third offense fine not to exceed $20000 andor public service time not to exceed 100 hours at the discretion of the court 4   secs 1638616413  reserved article xv  loitering definitions the following words terms and phrases when used in this article shall have the meanings ascribed to them in this section except where the context clearly indicates a different meaning public place means an area generally visible to the public view and includes streets sidewalks bridges alleys plazas parks driveways parking lots automobiles whether moving or not and buildings open to the general public including those which serve food or drink or provide entertainment and the doorways and entrances to buildings or dwellings and the ground enclosing them 1   loitering prohibited a general it shall be unlawful for any person to loiter or prowl in a place at a time or in a manner not usual for lawabiding individuals under circumstances that warrant a justifiable and reasonable alarm or immediate concern for the safety of persons or property in the vicinity among the circumstances which may be considered in determining whether such alarm or immediate concern is warranted is the fact that a person exhibiting suspicious behavior in a high crime area takes flight upon appearance of a law enforcement officer or manifestly endeavors to conceal himself or any object unless flight by the person or other circumstances makes it impracticable a law enforcement officer shall prior to any arrest for an offense under this section afford the person an opportunity to dispel any alarm or immediate concern which would otherwise be warranted by requesting him to identify and explain his presence and conduct no person shall be convicted of an offense under this section if the law enforcement officer did not comply with this procedure or if it appears at trial that the explanation given by the person is true and if believed by the officer at the time would have dispelled the alarm or immediate concern b disobedience to warning or posted noloitering signs it shall be unlawful for any person after first being warned by a law enforcement officer or where a noloitering sign or signs have been posted to loiter stand sit or lie in or upon any public or quasipublic sidewalk street curb crosswalk walkway area mall or that portion of private property utilized for public use so as to hinder or obstruct unreasonably the free passage of pedestrians or vehicles thereon  nor shall any person block or obstruct or prevent the free access to the entrance to any building open to the public c loitering near schools and colleges 1 it shall be unlawful and illegal for any person or persons to loiter within 500 feet distance of any school within the territorial limits of the city said distance shall be measured along the public thoroughfare to the nearest point of the school ground in use as part of the school facilities 2 it shall be unlawful and illegal for any person to loiter upon any school college or university grounds or within any school college or university building within the territorial limits of the city 3 a person shall be deemed guilty of loitering who remains in a school college or university building or upon the grounds thereof not having any reason or relationship involving custody of or responsibility for a pupil or any other specific legitimate reason for being upon such premises and not having written permission from anyone authorized to grant such permission d penalty any person violating the provisions of this section shall be deemed guilty of a misdemeanor and upon conviction shall be fined andor imprisoned as stated in this 2   secs 1641616443  reserved article xvi  wrecker rotation program purpose administration a to afford reasonable and prompt response time the city police department desires to utilize only the services of wrecker companies located within the corporate city limits or within five miles of the city that express a desire to participate in the departments wrecker rotation program wrecker companies desiring to participate must meet all the standard conditions and agree to comply with those conditions b the police departments rotation program is controlled and regulated by the chief of police establishment of requirements rules regulations and schedule of maximum fees for services participation in the program is on a strictly voluntary basis c wrecker companies applying for the right to participate in the rotation program freely and willingly subject themselves to compliance with the requirements rules regulations and schedule of maximum fees for services as established d the chief of police or his designee will administer the wrecker rotation program the designee upon approval of the chief shall have the authority to suspend a wrecker company from participating in the rotation program if it is found not to be in compliance with the requirements rules regulations and schedule of fees for authorized services 1   equipment requirements the wrecker shall be equipped with the following 1 each wrecker shall be equipped with oscillating rotating or flashing amber color emergency lights mounted on the cab or boom brace of the truck 2 each wrecker shall be equipped with a five pound or larger fire extinguisher rated for class a b and c fires the extinguisher shall be permanently mounted on the wrecker to ensure easy access the extinguisher must be annually certified and be fully charged or recharged as necessary 3 each wrecker shall carry as standard equipment tow sling tow bar towing dollies safety chains wrecker bar heavy duty broom shovel and container for debris and other equipment necessary to the safe and efficient operations of the wrecker 4 each wrecker and its equipment shall be modern and in excellent mechanical condition 5 any wrecker on the rotation list will be required to be registered with the city a if any wrecker or any of its equipment fails to meet the above requirements the designated officer will disapprove the wrecker company in that event the company may make repairs as needed and resubmit its requests b upon passing requirements all wrecker companies located within the corporate limits or ten miles of the city meeting the requirements of all city zoning rules regulations laws and upon issuance of a city business license may apply for inclusion on the departments rotation list c each wrecker service shall be required to inspect its wreckers and equipment monthly to ensure continuing compliance wreckers or equipment which do not pass requirements shall be taken out of operation by the wrecker service until such time as repairs are made or defective equipment has been repaired d in addition to the minimum requirements to conduct a wrecker business within the city rotation list applicants shall 1 provide wrecker and motor vehicle storage services to the city 24 hours a day seven days a week 2 arrive at the requested service location within 25 minutes of notification by the police department 3 remove any debris including but not limited to glass and parts from the accident scene where service is provided 4 maintain a fencedin motor vehicle storage facility area of sufficient size and design to ensure the secure storage of all motor vehicles towed there shall be an operator on call capable of responding to requests for wrecker service as well as an attendant available for the release of vehicles to the owner or responsible driver during normal business hours usually  am to  pm seven days a week if any vehicle storage facility is located outside the corporate limits it shall be within a reasonable distance to allow minimal inconvenience for owners of towed and stored vehicles wishing to pick up vehicles the determination of a reasonable distance will be solely at the discretion of the police department  however generally it would be within the 25 minutes response time area from any point within the city 5 the wrecker company shall take all necessary precautions to protect motor vehicles and personal property contained therein from theft or damage until property is released to the rightful owner the wrecker company shall be responsible for any theft vandalism or damage caused to vehicle towedstored 6 minimum standards for equipment i at least one wrecker of not less than one ton in size with dual rear wheels and booster brakes ii a power operated winch line and boom with a factory rated lifting capacity of not less than 8000 pounds single line capacity iii standard equipment tow sling wheel lifts or cradle devices towing dollies safety chains wrecker bars fire extinguishers flood lights to the rear heavy duty brooms shovels containers for debris and approved warning devices  insurance a any wrecker service on the rotation list shall carry liability insurance on its wreckers and its premises in an amount no less than $30000000 for a standard wrecker b any wrecker service on the rotation list shall carry garage keepers liability insurance covering customers vehicles in an amount no less than $10000000  right of entry reinspection the police department shall have the right at any time upon presentation of proper identification to enter into or upon any wrecker participating in the rotation program for the purpose of inspecting the wrecker and its equipment to ensure public safety and adherence to the provisions any wrecker or equipment which is found to be unsafe or in poor mechanical or physical condition shall be immediately taken out of service until repaired or replaced or reinspected by the designated officer of the police department  application selection  fees those wrecker firms that do not wish to participate in the program will not be used in the selection process the maximum fee for services by a licensed wrecker in the limits of the city or within 25 minutes of the city shall be established by the city council 1 towing and storage charges a operators fee for towing services rendered shall not exceed the maximum amounts as set forth in appendix a to the citys ordinances and as such amounts may be amended by the city council from time to time b these rates are the maximum allowed under this article this does not preclude charges of lesser amounts note all wrecker companies participating in the rotation program of the department agree to abide by the above list of charges for all services rendered in response to police calls for their tow services 2 stored or impounded vehicles a stored or impounded vehicles shall not be released until proper evidence of ownership is presented to the police department upon presentation the police department will issue a signed tow release to be given to the wrecker company for release of the vehicle the wrecker company is solely responsible for collection of all towing and storage fees b all rates approved by the city shall be posed in a conspicuous place at the business location of the wrecker company each vehicle owner shall be provided with an invoice or receipt itemizing all towing and storage charges when paid the city shall not be responsible for any towing or storage charges under any circumstance 3 general consideration a the wrecker company will be responsible for maintaining a compete record on each vehicle towed and stored monthly inventory reports containing all information may be requested by the city b the wrecker company shall obtain at its own expense any and all licenses permits and public liability insurance coverage c responsibility of the wrecker company any loss cost damage or other expense in performance of work under this agreement or occasioned by negligence of the wrecker company shall be the sole and entire responsibility of the wrecker company and not the city all and total liability shall be upon the towing company from initial hookup to a vehicle until release of said vehicle d the wrecker company agrees to indemnify and save harmless the city its employees agents and assigns from suit and claims or action of every nature and description brought for or on account of or sustained by any person or persons as a result of any act or acts of the wrecker company its employees agents or assigns in the performance of services under the terms of the contract  rotation list dispatching a the police dispatcher shall upon the request of the ownerdriver of a vehicle damaged or disabled on a streethighway or public place call any wrecker company having a business license issued by the city b if no particular wrecker company is requested by the vehicle ownerdriver the police dispatcher shall upon the direction of the investigating officer call a wrecker from the wrecker rotation list c no wrecker company will be able to tow for another company once called if wrecker is unable to respond the next wrecker on the rotation list will be called d wrecker companies unable to respond when called will forfeit the tow a notation will be entered on the rotation list the next wrecker on the list will be contacted to respond e after three consecutive forfeits the wrecker company will be taken off rotation list  police regulations a dummy companies and other interests it shall be unlawful for any owner or operator of a wrecker company to subcontract or have any connection association or agent of any company to drive or park along any streets or highways soliciting wrecker or towing services it shall be unlawful for any city employee to solicit business for any wrecker company it shall likewise be unlawful for any owner operator or agent of a towing company to entice or engage a city employee to solicit business for the service and upon conviction shall forfeit its eligibility to participate in the rotation program c use of emergency lights wrecker companies shall not operate any emergency lights except at the scene of an accident while hooking up to the vehicle to be towed or while actually towing a vehicle emergency lights shall not be operated while en route to any accident scene or other service call d miscellaneous 1 no wrecker shall be given or operated in a manner as to interfere with the duties of the police investigating accidents 2 direction of police officer shall be obeyed at all times and any licensed wrecker will promptly furnish service when requested to do so by the police in order to clear traffic and promote public safety e violations 1 all alleged violations of these authorized tow service requirements rules regulations and schedule or deviation from the terms or requirements of this article or a failure to provide service as stipulated herein may result in suspension from the rotation list or termination as deemed appropriate by terms and phrases when used in this solid waste code shall have the meanings ascribed to them in this section except where the context clearly indicates a different meaning bulky waste means large items such as furniture mattresses large auto parts trees branches stumps and other oversized wastes whose large size precludes or complicates their handling by normal collection processing or disposal methods commercial container means any container which a consists of four permanently attached sides and a bottom  b is made of metal durable plastic or other nonabsorbent material  c is freestanding  d is emptied or transported by mechanical means  and e is used to collect or store solid waste and include but are not limited to rollonrolloff boxes dumpsters compactors and similar receptacles used to collect solid waste commercial users means any commercial business including without limitation retail stores offices restaurants and warehouses  governmental and institutional offices and buildings including without limitation schools and hospitals  churches and other notforprofit organizations  hotels and motels  multifamily dwelling units that contain four or more units where solid waste is collected in a commercial container  mobile home parks where solid waste is collected in a commercial container  and agricultural and industrial facilities construction and wallboard and lumber from the construction renovation or demolition of a structure  and cardboard paper plastic wood and metal scraps from a construction renovation or demolition project commercial of future payment tree cuttings for wood lumber or building material of any sort including without limitation commercial landscaping land clearing and tree services  where such contractor exceeds the protection agency or appropriate agency of the state of south carolina the state to be hazardous as that term is defined by or pursuant to federal or state law or regulations residential user means i designated by the city for the collection of bagged solid waste or recyclables  which shall include the following 1 a residential roll cart which means a green roll cart for the collection of solid waste  and 2 a recycling roll cart which means a pink roll cart for the collection of recyclables small commercial user means small commercial enterprises including without limitation small retail stores and professional offices that generate solid waste in volumes comparable to residential users that may be reasonably accommodated use of solid waste roll carts designation as a small commercial user shall in all instances be in the sole discretion of the city pursuant to subsection 2023c of this solid waste code solid waste means waste resulting from the operation of residential commercial industrial governmental or institutional establishments that would normally be collected processed and disposed of public or private solid waste management service including without limitation putrescible waste such as animal fruit and vegetable matter and other organic refuse resulting from the handling preparation cooking and consumption of food to include cartons cans bottles or other containers associated with food consumption  animal offal and carcasses of less than ten pounds in weight except those slaughtered for human consumption  and refuse and rubbish incident to the normal conduct of a household or business and other trash such as bags paper paper boxes and containers sweepings other accumulations of a similar nature  and broken toys tools equipment and utensils  but does not include hazardous waste  bulky waste  white goods  yard debris  construction and demolition debris  medical waste generated in the diagnosis treatment or immunization of human beings or animals  solid or dissolved materials in domestic sewage  solid or dissolved materials in irrigation return flows  waste generated processes  industrial discharges  or similar waste solid waste service means and shall include the following 1 commercial solid waste service which means the collection and disposal of solid waste of commercial users from commercial containers  and 2 residential solid waste service which means the curbside collection and disposal of solid waste of residential users from residential roll carts white goods means discarded appliances water heaters freezers and other similar domestic and commercial large appliances  scrap metal copper and iron  and machinery and equipment yard debris means leaves grass clippings pine straw shrubbery brush limbs and other vegetative matter  1182016 provision of solid waste services generally the city shall collect and dispose of all solid waste generated within the city the city may at its discretion make use of city staff and equipment to provide solid waste services or contract with a private contractor to provide solid waste services on behalf of the city the provisions of this solid waste code shall apply regardless of whether the solid waste services are provided by the city or by a private contractor on the citys behalf provided however the enforcement of the provisions of this solid waste code shall be the responsibility of the city administrator or designee  1182016 placement of solid waste and recyclables all solid waste and recyclables shall be placed in either a roll cart or commercial container as applicable excess solid waste or recyclables shall not be placed on top of or outside of a roll cart of commercial container in the event that the volume of solid waste or recyclables generated by any user consistently exceeds the capacity of such users container or the frequency of such users service the city may make necessary adjustments to container size or number or the frequency of service and adjust the fees charged to such user accordingly no person shall deposit solid waste or any other form of trash garbage refuse waste or yard debris into a commercial container except those commercial users authorized for the use thereof  1182016 residential solid waste service  small commercial users a residential solid waste service shall be provided by the city to each residential user once per week on a schedule to be determined by the city in order to receive residential solid waste service all solid waste must be placed in a solid waste roll cart and placed at the curb by  am on the scheduled day of service b each residential user in the city shall be charged a monthly fee for residential solid waste service based upon the number of solid waste roll carts that have been provided to each residential user fees for residential solid waste service shall be billed along with billing for utility service and which shall be due and payable and subject to penalties for nonpayment in the same manner as fees for utility service fees for residential solid waste service shall be established by the council and may be amended from time to time the city may use any legal or equitable remedy to collect unpaid fees for residential solid waste service c commercial enterprises that produce volumes of solid waste that are comparable to that of residential users may request designation as a small commercial user small commercial users shall be subject to the provisions of this solid waste code that pertain to residential solid waste service and shall be charged for solid waste service based upon the fees set for residential users commercial enterprises may request designation as a small commercial user by contacting the city administrator and the city may in its discretion approve such requests as appropriate  1182016 recycling service a residential users that wish to receive recycling service may request a recycling roll cart by contacting the city or a private contractor designated by the city at the contact phone number provided on the citys website recycling service shall be provided by the city to each such residential user once every second week on a schedule to be determined by the city in order to receive recycling service all recyclables must be placed in a recycling roll cart and placed at the curb by  am on the scheduled day of service b each residential user shall be entitled to receive recycling service using one recycling roll cart at no additional charge  provided however that council may impose a fee for such recycling service at any time for each additional recycling roll cart provided each such residential user shall be charged a monthly fee for recycling service fees for recycling service shall be billed along with billing for utility service and which shall be due and payable and subject to penalties for nonpayment in the same manner as fees for utility service fees for recycling service shall be established by the council and may be amended from time to time the city may use any legal or equitable remedy to collect unpaid fees for recycling service  1182016 roll carts a roll carts shall not be placed 1 further than three feet from the edge of the curb street or roadway  2 in front of or adjacent to a mailbox so as to interfere with the delivery of mail  or 3 placed in or left in any driveway or roadway so as to inhibit ingress or egress or otherwise block traffic or cause a traffic hazard b roll carts may be placed at the curb no earlier than  pm on the day prior to the scheduled day of service and shall be removed from the curb no later than  pm on the scheduled day of service c each residential user shall be provided one solid waste roll cart and upon request one recycling roll cart at no cost in the event that the volume of solid waste or recyclables exceeds the capacity of the respective roll cart additional roll carts may be requested by contacting the city or a private contractor designated by the city at the contact phone number provided on the citys website additional roll carts shall be provided at the thencurrent cost to the city of such roll cart which shall be added to the monthly bill and monthly fees charged to the residential user shall thereafter be adjusted accordingly if the city determines that the volume of solid waste or recyclables of a residential user consistently exceeds the volume of the respective roll cart the city may in its discretion provide additional roll carts charge the costs therefor and adjust the monthly fees for residential solid waste or recycling service accordingly d in the event that any roll cart is in need of replacement due to normal wear and tear or for other reasons that do not constitute willful damage to or loss of a roll cart such roll cart shall be replaced at no cost  provided however that council may in its discretion impose a fee for replacement roll carts at any time in the event that any roll cart is in need of replacement due to reasons that constitute willful damage to or loss of a roll cart the residential user shall be billed the thencurrent cost to the city of replacing such roll cart e in no case shall an address owners names or any other information stickers or other material be painted written or otherwise placed on any roll cart a violation of this provision may result in the residential user being billed the thencurrent cost to the city of any such roll cart  1182016 backdoor service backdoor solid waste or recycling service will be provided at no additional cost to residential users where it is determine by the city that no individual residing in a residence is physically capable of moving the roll cart to the curb individuals may apply for backdoor service by contacting the city administrator  1182016 commercial solid waste service a commercial users and the city shall mutually agree on the size commercial container and the weekly frequency of commercial solid waste service that is appropriate for the commercial user given the volume of solid waste produced by the commercial user commercial solid waste service shall be provided on a weekly basis at the agreed upon frequency on a schedule to be determined by the city the city may in its discretion increase the container size or the frequency of commercial solid waste service in the event that the volumes of solid waste produced exceed the capacity of the thencurrent arrangement b each commercial user shall be charged a monthly fee for commercial solid waste service based upon the size of the commercial container and the frequency of commercial solid waste service commercial users who choose to make use of an outside collector for the collection of solid waste shall be charged a minimum fee for the availability of solid waste service c fees for commercial solid waste service shall be billed along with billing for utility service and which shall be due and payable and subject to penalties for nonpayment in the same manner as fees for utility service fees for commercial solid waste service and a minimum fee for the availability of solid waste service shall be established by the council and may be amended from time to time the city may use any legal or equitable remedy to collect unpaid fees for commercial solid waste service  1182016 commercial containers a commercial containers shall be placed at locations that are mutually acceptable to the city and the commercial user and that are otherwise in compliance with the citys land use ordinances  provided however that the city may make the final determination as to the placement of any commercial container in the event that the parties are unable to reach an agreement b commercial containers shall be provided at no additional cost in the size agreed upon between the commercial user and the city and in the event that any commercial container is in need of replacement due to normal wear and tear or for other reasons that do not constitute willful damage to or loss of the commercial container such commercial container shall be replaced at no cost  provided however that council may in its discretion impose a fee for new or replacement commercial containers at any time in the event that any commercial container is in need of replacement due to reasons that constitute willful damage to or loss of the commercial container the commercial user shall be billed the thencurrent cost to the city of replacing such commercial container c in no case shall an address owners names business name or any other information stickers or other material be painted written or otherwise placed on any commercial container that is owned by the city or by a private contractor retained by the city to provide solid waste services a violation of this provision may result in the commercial user being billed the thencurrent cost to the city of any such commercial container d commercial users shall keep the commercial containers lids and doors closed to prevent rainwater flies rodents and wild animals from entering the commercial container and to prevent solid waste from blowing out of the commercial container  1182016 waste excluded from solid waste service a solid waste service does not include the collection or disposal of large volumes of waste resulting from a flood storm fire or other natural or manmade disaster the city may collect and dispose of such waste on a case by case basis and may charge users for such service b the city shall not collect white goods bulky waste hazardous waste construction or demolition debris or any other form of waste not specifically addressed under this solid waste code in the event that such items are placed for collection the city will notify the individual or business listed upon the propertys utility bill or if no utility service is provided to such property the individual listed in the property tax records that such items or other material are to be removed within 48 hours failure to do so shall be considered a violation of this solid waste code  1182016 yard debris generally a the city shall collect yard debris in typical household quantities subject to the conditions of this solid waste code that are generated from typical lawn or garden care performed by a property owner or occupant or by a hired man the city shall collect yard debris on an asneeded basis in as expeditiously as possible given the varying volumes of yard debris generated throughout the city in different seasons b the city shall not collect yard debris generated from work performed by commercial contractors or resulting from contracted land clearing work such yard debris must be removed by the commercial contractor performing the work or by the property owner or occupant c yard debris is to be placed at the front property line or curb for collection by the city yard debris shall not be placed in or on any storm drain gutter street or sidewalk or placed in such a way so as to cause a traffic hazard d raking blowing or scattering yard debris clippings other loose natural materials or parking lot debris onto a sidewalk or adjacent property or into a street is prohibited such action shall be considered littering and shall subject to all applicable fines and penalties  1182016 collection of yard debris a yard debris will be collected by the city provided that the following conditions are met 1 all leaves pine straw grass clippings brush and other loose yard debris must be bagged and separated from all other yard debris  2 limbs cuttings larger shrubbery and similar natural materials are not to exceed three inches in diameter and six feet in length and must be separated from all other yard debris  3 smaller brush limbs and cuttings are to be piled together and must be separated from other yard debris  4 yard debris must have been generated on the property from which they are being collected  and 5 yard debris may not be mixed with other types of waste such as solid waste bulky waste or construction or demolition debris  b yard debris collected or generated as a result of the clearing of a vacant lot will not be collected by the city and is to be removed by the landowner or his designated representative c logs limbs and similar natural materials larger than three inches in diameter and six feet in length  rocks dirt sand or similar materials  stumps and other bulky items will not be collected by the city and must be disposed of by the property owner or occupant d in the event that yard debris other vegetative or natural materials or other waste are placed for collection in violation of the provisions of this section the city will not collect any such items or waste in such event the city will notify the individual or business listed upon the propertys utility bill or if no utility service is provided to such property the individual listed in the property tax records that such material is to be removed within 48 hours failure to do so shall be considered a violation of this solid waste code  1182016 enforcement  penalty for violation of chapter a for the purposes of enforcing the provisions of this chapter notice of violation shall be issued by police officers codes enforcement officers or any other person authorized to enforce municipal ordinances b whenever a police officer or codes enforcement officer observes a violation of this solid waste code he shall hand to the violator or leave upon or affix to the premises where the violation occurred a uniform ordinance summons such ordinance summons shall bear the date time and nature of the violation the identity of the violator when known the address of the violator or the address where the violation occurred the amount of bond to be remitted in response to the ordinance summons the time date and place of trial for the violation and shall be signed by the official issuing the ordinance summons and bear the identification number of such official c any such person found guilty of violating this article shall be fined or imprisoned or both no less than $10000 or no more than $50000 plus authorized costs and assessments or no less than five days or no more than 30 days in prison any monetary fine shall include properly assessable costs as required and permitted by law  1182016 exception for producers of solid waste this solid waste code shall not prohibit the actual producers of solid waste or the owners of property upon which solid waste has accumulated from personally collecting conveying and disposing of such solid waste provided such producers and owners otherwise comply with the provisions of this solid waste code and with any other governing law or ordinances a minimum fee will still be charged for the availability of solid waste service  1182016 exception for outside collectors and haulers of solid waste no outside collector or hauler of solid waste or any other type of waste from outside of the city shall convey such waste over the citys streets unless such collectors or haulers comply with the provisions of this solid waste code and with any other governing law or ordinances this solid waste code shall not prohibit outside collectors or haulers from providing solid waste or other waste collection services within the city provided that such collector or hauler seek the permission of the city which may in the citys discretion be given in the form of a nonexclusive franchise use of an outside collector or hauler shall not exempt the user thereof from the payment of a minimum fee for the availability of solid waste service  1182016 secs 20352057  reserved article iii  litter short title this article shall be known and may be cited as the lake city antilitter  1   1170 definitions the following words terms and phrases when used in this article shall have the meanings ascribed to them in this section except where the context clearly indicates a different meaning authorized private receptacle means a litter storage and collection receptacle as required and authorized in this means putrescible animal and vegetable wastes resulting from the handling preparation cooking and consumption of food litter garbage refuse and rubbish mean all other waste material which if thrown or deposited as herein prohibited tends to create a danger to public health safety and welfare park means a park reservation playground beach recreation center or any other public area in the city owned or used by the city and devoted to active or passive recreation private premises means any dwelling house building or other structure designed or used either wholly or in part for private residential purposes whether inhabited or temporarily or continuously uninhabited or vacant and shall include any yard grounds walk driveway porch steps vestibule or mailbox belonging or appurtenant to such dwelling house building or other structure public place means any and all streets sidewalks boulevards alleys or other public ways and any and all public parks squares spaces grounds and buildings refuse means all putrescible and nonputrescible solid wastes except body wastes including garbage rubbish ashes street cleanings dead animals abandoned automobiles and solid market and industrial wastes rubbish means nonputrescible solid wastes consisting of both combustible and noncombustible wastes such as paper wrappings cigarettes cardboard tin cans yard clippings leaves wood glass bedding crockery and similar materials vehicle means every device in upon or by which any person or property is or may be transported or drawn upon a highway including devices used exclusively upon stationary rails or tracks 2   1171 litter in public places for addition regulations concerning litter on sidewalks see section 2230 no person shall throw or deposit litter in or upon any street sidewalk or other public place within the city except in public receptacles in authorized private receptacles for collection or in official city dumps 3   1172 placement of litter in receptacles so as to prevent scattering persons placing litter in public receptacles or in authorized private receptacles shall do so in such a manner as to prevent it from being carried or deposited by the elements upon any street sidewalk or other public place or upon private property 4   1173 sweeping litter into gutters prohibited no person shall sweep into or deposit in any gutter street or other public place within the city the accumulation of litter from any building or lot or from any public or private sidewalk or driveway persons owning or occupying property shall keep the sidewalk in front of their premises free of litter 5   1174 merchants duty to keep sidewalks free of litter no person owning or occupying a place of business shall sweep into or deposit in any gutter street or other public place within the city the accumulation of litter from any building or lot or from any public or private sidewalk or driveway persons owning or occupying places of business within the city shall keep the sidewalk in front of their business premises free of litter 6   1175 litter thrown by persons in vehicles no person while a driver or passenger in a vehicle shall throw or deposit litter upon any street or other public place within the city or upon private property 7   1176 truck loads causing litter no person shall drive or move any truck or other vehicle within the city unless such vehicle is so constructed or loaded as to prevent any load contents or litter from being blown or deposited upon any street alley or other public place nor shall any person drive or move any vehicle or truck within the city the wheels or tires of which carry onto or deposit in any street alley or other public place mud dirt sticky substances litter or foreign matter of any kind 8   1177 litter in parks no person shall throw or deposit litter in any park within the city except in public receptacles and in such a manner that the litter will be prevented from being carried or deposited by the elements upon any part of the park or upon any street or other public place where public receptacles are not provided all such litter shall be carried away from the park by the person responsible for its presence and properly disposed of elsewhere as provided herein 9   1178 litter on occupied private property no person shall throw or deposit litter on any private property within the city whether owned by such person or not except that the owner or person in control of private property may maintain authorized private receptacles for collection in such a manner that litter will be prevented from being carried or deposited by the elements upon any street sidewalk or other public place or upon any private property 10   1180 owner to maintain premises free of litter the owner or person in control of any private property shall at all times maintain the premises free of litter  provided however that this section shall not prohibit the storage of litter in authorized private receptacles for collection 11   1181 litter on vacant lots no person shall throw or deposit litter on any open or vacant private property within the city whether owned by such person or not 12   1182 clearing of litter from open private property by city a notice to remove  the city code enforcement officer is hereby authorized and empowered to notify the owner of any open or vacant private property within the city or the agent of such owner to properly dispose of litter located on such owners property which is dangerous to public health safety or welfare such notice shall be by registered mail addressed to the owner at his last known address b action upon noncompliance  upon the failure neglect or refusal of any owner or agency so notified to properly dispose of litter dangerous to the public health safety or welfare within 15 days after receipt of written notice provided for in subsection a of this section or within 15 days after the date of such notice in the event the same is returned to the city post office department because of its inability to make delivery thereof provided the same was properly addressed to the last known address of such owner or agent the code enforcement officer is hereby authorized and empowered to pay for the disposing of such litter or to order its disposal by the city c charge included in tax bill  when the city has effected the removal of such dangerous litter or has paid for its removal the actual cost thereof plus accrued interest at the rate of six percent per annum from the date of the completion of the work if not paid by such owner prior thereto shall be charged to the owner of such property on the next regular tax bill forwarded to such owner by the city and said charge shall be due and payable by said owner at the time of payment of such bill d recorded statement constitutes lien  where the full amount due the city is not paid by such owner within five days after the disposal of such litter as provided for in subsections a and b of this section then and in that case the city code enforcement officer shall cause to be recorded with the city finance director a sworn statement showing the cost and expense incurred for the work the date the work was done and the location of the property on which said work was done the recordation of such sworn statement shall constitute a lien and privilege on the property and shall remain in full force and effect for the amount due in principal and interest plus costs of court if any for collection until final payment has been made said costs and expenses shall be collected in the manner fixed by law for the collection of taxes and further shall be subject to a delinquent penalty of five percent in the event same is not paid in full on or before the date the tax bill upon which said charge appears becomes delinquent sworn statements recorded in accordance with the provisions shall be prima facie evidence that all legal formalities have been complied with and that the work has been done properly and satisfactorily and shall be full notice to every person concerned that the amount of the statement plus interest constitutes a charge against the property designated or described in the statement and that the same is due and collectible as provided by law 13   1183 penalties any person violating any of the provisions of this article shall be deemed guilty of a misdemeanor and upon conviction thereof shall be liable to the penalty stated in section 18 14   1184 secs 20722099  reserved article iv  donation receptacles definition donation receptacle means any unattended container box or similar device that is used for soliciting and collecting donations including but not limited to clothing footwear books and other salvageable household goods  9132016 conditions for placement of donation receptacle any donation receptacle located on any property within the city must comply with the following regulations 1 donation receptacles shall either be placed along the side or rear of any property and shall be located within side or rear setback area of such property as set forth in the citys zoning ordinance the donation receptacle shall be situated on the property so as to not interfere with sighttriangles or onsite circulation or any bufferyards landscaping parking or any other elements of the design of a site that are required pursuant to the citys zoning ordinance or that may have been imposed as part of the site plan approval for the premises 2 donation receptacles shall not be placed within a designated parking space 3 donation receptacles shall not be placed in such a manner as to cause an obstruction for pedestrians or motorists 4 only one donation receptacle shall be permitted per lot and shall only be permitted on properties that contain a primary permitted use pursuant to the citys zoning ordinance 5 donation receptacles shall not exceed six and onehalf feet in height 6 signage on donation receptacles shall not exceed fiveinch letter height 7 the following information must be clearly and conspicuously displayed on the exterior of the donation receptacle the name and address of the property owner who owns the donation receptacle and the name of any entity which may share profit or benefit from any donations collected via the donation receptacle  9132016 donation receptacle maintenance donation receptacles shall be maintained in good condition and appearance with no structural damage holes or visible rust and shall be kept free of graffiti all donation receptacles shall be free of debris and shall be serviced regularly so as to prevent overflow of donations or the accumulation of junk debris or other material all donation receptacles must be securely locked to prevent unauthorized individuals from being able to open or enter the donation receptacle  9132016 notice of violation and fine in the event that any property within the city has upon it any donation receptacle that violates the provisions of this article the owner of such property shall be served with written notice of the violation and in the event that the violation is not corrected within 30 days of service of such notice the owner of such property shall be issued a uniform ordinance summons notice of the violation shall be served upon the owners of the property at the owners last known address by first class mail postage prepaid or served personally by an official of the city the written notice shall include a detailed description of the violations located on the property  9132016 streets sidewalks and other public property footnotes  1  state law
