1   31 list of definitions the following words terms and phrases when used in this chapter shall have the meanings ascribed to them in this section except where the context clearly indicates a different meaning collector street means those streets which serve as feeders to a major street as collectors of traffic from minor streets and for circulation around a residential neighborhood culdesac means a dead end street where there is room for a vehicle to turn at a circular end master plan and comprehensive plan mean any part or element of the overall plan for development adopted by the planning commission as provided by the general assembly of the state of south carolina street means relates to and includes streets and avenues boulevards roads highways expressways lanes alleys and other ways for the purpose of this chapter streets are classified by function as follows major street means those indicated as such on the major thoroughfare plan map which serve primarily as major traffic ways for travel within the city minor street means those streets provided for the primary purpose of furnishing access to abutting properties subdivider means an individual firm association syndicate partnership corporation trust or any other legal entity or agent therefor that undertakes the activities covered by these regulations inasmuch as the subdivision plat is merely a necessary means to the end of assuring a satisfactory development the term subdivider is intended to include the terms developer and builder even though the persons involved in successive stages of the project may vary subdivision means and shall be construed to be a division of a tract or parcel of land into two or more lots building sites or divisions for the purpose whether immediate or future of conveyance transfer improvement sale legacy or building development and includes all division of land involving a new street or a change in existing streets and includes resubdivision and where appropriate to the context relates to the process of subdividing or to the land or areas subdivided  provided however that the following are not included within this definition 1 the combination or recombination of portions of previously platted lots where the total number of lots is not increased and the resultant lots are equal to the standards set forth in this chapter 2 the division of land into parcels of five acres or more where no new street is involved 2   31 preapplication consultation whenever the subdivision of a tract of land within the city is proposed the subdivider is urged to consult early and informally with the planning commission the subdivider may submit sketch plans and data showing existing conditions within the site and its vicinity and the proposed layout and development of the subdivision the purpose of the preapplication review is to facilitate the subsequent preparation of plans and no fees are charged for this review   art iv secs 3483432  reserved article ii  preliminary plat submission of plat following the preapplication consultation of a proposed land subdivision the subdivider shall submit to the planning commission the following 1 the preliminary plat and other documents as specified hereafter  2 a letter requesting review and approval of the preliminary plat and giving the name and address of a person to whom the notice of a hearing by the planning commission on the preliminary plat shall be sent  and 3 a preliminary plat filing fee as set forth in appendix a to the citys ordinances and as it may be amended by the city council from time to time unless the plat contains five or less lots in which case the fee shall be an amount as established from time to time per lot 1   51 review of preliminary plat a the planning commission shall review the preliminary plat for conformance to the rules and regulations of this article and the requirements of the zoning chapter and shall take into consideration the general requirements of the community and the best use of the land to be subdivided b copies of plats shall also be furnished to the planning commission for distribution to the county health department state health department state highway department county board of education city fire department and city postmaster these departments agencies boards and officers may review the preliminary plat and submit written comments to the planning commission on the proposed subdivision with respect to their specific standards ordinances regulations andor policies such comments will be reviewed and evaluated by the planning commission prior to a decision on the proposed subdivision c the preliminary plat may be approved disapproved or approved subject to modifications the commission may indicate the specific changes required and the public improvements which must be provided as required by this article or the amount of the performance bond therefor which it will require as a prerequisite to the approval of the final plat 2   52 notice and hearing on preliminary plat the planning commission shall hold a hearing on the preliminary plat within 30 days of submission notice of the time and place of which shall be sent by the secretary of the planning commission by registered or certified mail to the person designated in the letter requesting preliminary plat review and approval not less than five days before the date fixed therefor if action is not taken within 30 days of the date of submission the preliminary plat shall be considered approved and a certificate of approval issued on demand the subdivider may waive the 30 day time limit and consent to an extension of time 3   53 tentative and conditional nature of preliminary plat approval tentative and conditional approval of a preliminary plat shall not constitute approval of the final plat rather it shall be deemed an expression of approval of the layout submitted on the preliminary plat as a guide to the preparation of the final plat which will be submitted for approval of the planning commission and for recording upon fulfillment of the requirements of these regulations and the stipulations in the conditional approval if any 4   54 expiration of tentative approval of preliminary plat the tentative approval shall expire after one year unless an extension of time is granted by the planning commission 5   55 preliminary plat specifications the preliminary plat shall meet the following requirements 1 number of copies  eight copies of the preliminary plat shall be furnished by the subdivider  one copy to be retained in the files of the planning commission copies to be reviewed by appropriate city county and state officials and the postmaster and one copy to be returned to the subdivider 2 form  the preliminary plat shall be drawn clearly and legibly at a scale of one inch equals 100 feet or larger the sheet size shall not be less than 16 inches by 24 inches if the complete plat cannot be shown on one sheet it maybe shown on more than one sheet with an index map on a separate sheet of the same size 6   56 data required on preliminary plat the preliminary plat shall contain the following information 1 proposed subdivision name or identifying title and acreage to be subdivided 2 name and address of owner of record subdivider and owners of adjoining property 3 date graphic scale and north point 4 contours at an interval of not greater than one foot and such street cross sections and profiles as may be required by the planning commission where the land is relatively flat spot elevations at intervals sufficient to show the drainage pattern shall be plotted elevations of monuments or other permanent fixed points shall be noted 5 exact boundaries of the tract to be subdivided by distances and bearings 6 existing and proposed easements and their approximate location width and distances 7 names and dimensions of existing and proposed streets and alleys on and adjacent to the tract see section 3476 8 location and type of existing and proposed sewerage and storm drainage and water supply facilities and other utilities on or adjacent to the tract showing proposed connections detailed engineering information shall be submitted on adequacy of existing underground utilities 9 lot lines with approximate dimensions and lot numbers 10 accurate designation of natural water courses and proposed changes 11 engineering data regarding extent of areas subject to flooding and proposed solutions and finish grades see section 3471 12 sites if any and their acreages to be reserved or dedicated for public use 13 present zoning classification 14 vicinity map showing location of subdivision and its relationship to the rest of the city and surrounding countryside this may be shown at a smaller scale 7   57 secs 34403466  reserved article iii  subdivision standards and requirements general requirements and design standards for subdivisions subdividers shall observe the following general requirements and design standards of land subdivision in this article  conformance to major thoroughfare plan all streets and other features of the major thoroughfare plan shall be platted by the subdivider in the location and to the dimensions indicated on the major thoroughfare plan adopted by the planning commission 1   61 public sites and open spaces a when a proposed school site or other public building site park or other land for public uses is located in whole or in part in the subdivision the planning commission may require that as a prerequisite to plat approval such sites shall be dedicated or reserved by the subdivider for acquisition by the appropriate public agency b areas for parks playgrounds or other public uses shall be of reasonable size no arbitrary percentage of areas shall be insisted upon by the planning commission but in general developers should set aside not less than five percent of the area for these purposes c whenever a plat proposes the dedication of land to public use that the planning commission finds not required or suitable for such public use the planning commission shall refuse to approve the plat d the approval of a plat by the planning commission shall not be deemed to constitute or effect an acceptance by the city of the dedication of any street or other grounds shown upon the plat 2   62 subdivision names the name of the subdivision shall not duplicate or too closely approximate the name of any other subdivision within the city 3   63 suitability of land land subject to flooding and land deemed by the commission to be uninhabitable shall not be platted for residential occupancy nor for such other uses as may increase danger to health life or property or aggravate the flood hazard but such land within the plat shall be set aside for such uses as shall not be endangered by periodic or occasional inundation or shall not produce unsatisfactory living conditions 4   64 large parcels in case a tract is subdivided into larger parcels than ordinary building lots such parcels shall be arranged so as to allow the opening of future streets and logical future resubdivisions 5   65 shall front upon a public street lot lines shall be generally perpendicular or radial to street lines lot dimensions shall meet the requirements of the comprehensive zoning ordinance for the district or districts in which the subdivision is located corner lots shall be increased in size wherever necessary so as to provide that any structure to be placed thereon shall conform to the minimum setback line of each street as required in the comprehensive zoning ordinance 6   66 blocks the length shall not exceed 1200 feet or be less than 300 feet and the width sufficient to provide for two tiers of lots but irregularly shaped lots indented by culdesac streets and containing interior parks will be acceptable when properly designed and provision made for maintenance of interior parks 7   67 streets a conformance to thoroughfare plan and other elements of the master plan the arrangements of streets in the subdivision shall provide for the continuation of the principal streets in adjoining subdivisions or for their proper projection when adjoining property has not yet been subdivided and in general conform to the master plan b street names street names shall require the approval of the planning commission streets that are obviously in alignment with streets already existing and named shall be given the name of the existing street names of new streets shall not duplicate or closely approximate those of existing streets c street jogs street jogs with centerline or offsets of less than 125 feet shall not be permitted d existing street jogs where development is proposed on an existing street which jogs or offsets less than 125 feet such streets shall be realigned before development is permitted e dead end or culdesac streets the planning commission shall determine the length of dead end or culdesac streets they shall be provided at the closed end with a turnaround having a property line radius of at least 60 feet with an outside pavement radius of at least 50 feet f alleys alleys may be required at the rear of all lots used for multifamily commercial or industrial developments but shall not be provided in one and twofamily residential developments unless the subdivider provides evidence satisfactory to the planning commission of the need for alleys g reserve strips reserve strips controlling access to streets alleys and public grounds shall not be permitted unless the control is placed in the hands of the city council under conditions approved by the planning commission h street intersections street intersections shall be as nearly at right angles as possible no street intersection shall be at an angle of less than 60 degrees unless required by unusual circumstances i curb radii curb radii at street intersections shall be at least 25 feet where the angle of the street intersection is less than 90 degrees a radius of at least 30 feet shall be required j easements easements across lots or centered on rear or side lot lines shall be provided where necessary for utilities or drainage k double frontage lots except under special conditions double frontage lots shall be avoided where the planning commission under special conditions permits double frontage lots the frontage along the rear lot lines shall be screened with a masonry wall or evergreen hedge at least five feet in height 8   68 geometric standards and other shall not commence until the preliminary plat has been approved  intro improvements installed by subdivider the subdivider shall be required to install or have installed at his expense the following improvements 1 monuments two concrete monuments at least 36 inches in length and four inches square with a suitable center point at each street intersection on the rightofway line and iron pin monuments threefourths inch in diameter and 24 inches long at all points on boundary lines of lots where there is a change in direction and at all lot corners 2 streets all streets shall be paved according to the following specifications a minimum of at least 112 inches of hot plant mix asphalt shall be provided on a base of at least six inches thickness of compacted class a or b sand clay or topsoil or equivalent as specified by the state highway department no final grading or paving of the street or construction or installation of utilities in the bed of a street shall be permitted until the grade has been officially established no paving shall begin until the compacted base has been inspected and approved by the official representative of the city and underground utilities installed and approved 3 water mains water shall be provided according to the following specifications where a public water main is within 1500 feet of the subdivision at its nearest point the subdivider shall connect with such water main in such cases mains of at least six inches shall be required the subdivider shall be responsible for the costs of all taps and extensions to existing municipal facilities where a public water main is not reasonably accessible as determined by the planning commission the subdivider shall provide an individual water supply according to the standards of the city or the county health department and the most restrictive standard shall apply 4 sanitary sewers sanitary sewers shall be provided according to the following specifications wherever a public sanitary sewer is within 1500 feet of the subdivision at its nearest point and connection by gravity flow is feasible the subdivider shall connect with such sanitary sewer and provide a connection for each lot the size of the mains shall be at least eight inches the subdivider shall be responsible for the costs of all taps lift pump stations manholes and extensions to existing municipal facilities where sanitary sewers are not available an oxidation pond septic tank or other disposal device designed and installed according to standards of the city or the county health department may be permitted and the most restrictive standards shall apply 5 drainage storm sewers including open ditches and rightsofway shall be provided for the proper drainage of all surface water and shall be approved by the city engineer 6 variances or other improvements where the subdivider can show that a provision of these regulations would cause unnecessary hardship if strictly adhered to and where because of topographical or other conditions peculiar to the site in the opinion of the planning commission a departure may be made without destroying the intent of such provisions the planning commission may authorize a variance likewise if because of peculiar conditions or circumstances relative to a particular subdivision the planning commission may require the installation of sidewalks street trees or other improvements any variance thus authorized or additional improvement thus required is to be stated in writing in the minutes of the planning commission with the reasoning on which the variance or addition was justified set forth 7 reimbursement any subdivider person or other legal entity who may have been entitled to reimbursement under said as originally adopted shall not be entitled to any viii procedure for final plat approval the subdivider shall submit to the planning commission the following 1 the final plat and other documents as specified hereafter 2 a letter requesting a review and approval of the final plat and giving the name and address of a person to whom the notice of a hearing by the planning commission on the final plat shall be sent 1   81 review of final plat the planning commission shall review the final plat for conformance with the tentatively approved preliminary plat and with the rules and regulations of this article the final plat may be approved disapproved or approved subject to modifications 2   82 notice of hearing on final plat the planning commission shall hold a hearing on the final plat within 30 days of submission notice of the time and place of which shall be sent by the secretary of the planning commission by registered or certified mail to the person designated in the letter and on the plat requesting review and approval not less than five days before the date fixed therefor after the hearing notation of the action taken shall be made on each of three required copies of the final plat if action is not taken within 30 days of the date of submission the final plat shall be considered approved and a certificate of approval issued on demand the subdivider may waive the 30 day limit and consent to an extension of time the ground of disapproval of any plat shall be stated in the records of the planning commission 3   83 recording of final plat upon approval of the final plat with the signature of the secretary thereon the developer shall have the plat recorded in the office of the clerk of common pleas and general sessions of the county the subdivider shall have responsibility for payment of the recording fee 4 monuments 2 exact locations widths and names of all streets and alleys within and immediately adjoining the plat 3 street centerlines showing angles of deflection angles of intersection radii and lengths of tangents 4 lot lines with dimensions to the nearest onetenth foot and bearings 5 in numerical order and blocks lettered alphabetically 6 locations and dimensions of all improvements constructed or installed 7 private covenants or restrictions if any shall either be recorded on the final plat or on an identified document attached to the final plat 5   85 secs 3410834127  reserved article v  enforcement and penalties plat approval after this chapter shall have been put into effect any subdivision that fails to meet the requirements of this chapter shall be disapproved by the planning commission 1   91 recording of plats no plat of a subdivision lying within the corporate limits of the city shall be recorded in the office of the clerk of the court of common pleas and general sessions of the county unless it has been given final approval by the planning commission and the description by metes and bounds on the instrument of transfer or other document shall not exempt the transaction from such requirements the recording of a plat of a subdivision that has not been given final approval by the planning commission shall be a misdemeanor no plat shall be recorded that does not bear the signature and seal of a registered land surveyor 2   92 sale or transfer of lots the subdivider of any land within the city who transfers or sells or agrees to sell or negotiates to sell such land by reference to or exhibition of or by other use of a plat of subdivision of such land before such plat has been approved by the planning commission and recorded in the office of the clerk of the court of common pleas and general sessions of the county shall be guilty of a misdemeanor 3   93 acceptance of streets no public authority shall accept improve or maintain any street not shown on an approved and recorded final plat unless such street has received the legal status of a public street any street on an existing or proposed state highway department plan shall also be approved by the highway department prior to acceptance by the city see section 3434 4 building permit no building permit shall be issued and no building or other structure shall be erected on any lot within the city unless the street giving access to the lots is a public street any building erected in violation of these provisions is an unlawful structure and the code enforcement official city attorney or other agency of the city shall enjoin such erection or cause the building to be vacated or removed 5   95 secs 3413334162  reserved article vi  legal status provisions conflict with other laws when the provisions of this chapter specify more restrictive standards than required by any other statute the requirements of this chapter shall govern whenever the provisions of any other statute require more restrictive standards the provisions of such statute shall govern 1   101 manufactured homes footnotes  1  state law reference mobile and manufactured home parks sc   manufactured housing construction and safety standards sc   manufactured home installation requirements sc   used manufactured home minimum habitability requirements sc  article i  in general title and enactment the regulations set forth by this chapter shall be known as the mobile home lake city south carolina pursuant to the authority of police power conferred upon the city by the south carolina laws to act in behalf of the public health safety and welfare of its citizens the city council hereby adopts and enacts into law the lake city mobile home   art 1 jurisdiction and application this chapter shall apply within the city it shall be unlawful to locate develop construct operate expand or enlarge any mobile home park subdivision or mobile home without meeting the regulations and minimum requirements of this chapter   art 1 purpose the regulations herein for mobile homes are made pursuant to the citys police power to act in behalf and execute those actions deemed reasonable and necessary to enhance the health safety and welfare in the public interest of the citizens of the city this chapter has been prepared in consideration of the land use plan in order to determine suitable and nonsuitable locations for mobile homes mobile home parks and mobile home subdivisions the chapter has been developed to meet the following specific objectives and to ensure the quality of development 1 improve housing opportunities in the city by ensuring that mobile homes mobile home parks and mobile home subdivisions are located and developed under conditions that would not diminish environmental quality adversely affect other land and property values nor jeopardize the health and living conditions of the residents 2 minimize the governments cost for development and maintenance of public water and sewer systems fire protection and other government services by encouraging the location of mobile home parks and mobile home subdivisions to be in proximity to the source of such services rather than dispersed 3 ensure that mobile homes meet the minimum standards of all other state and city laws governing mobile homes mobile home parks or mobile home subdivisions   art 1 definitions the following words terms and phrases when used in this chapter shall have the meanings ascribed to them in this section except where the context clearly indicates a different meaning abandoned mobile home means a mobile home that has been unoccupied for one year or is not healthful or safe for occupancy and shows evidence of abandonment also a mobile home that both exhibits evidence of deterioration that would require repairs in excess of 50 percent of its current replacement value and is unoccupied ansi means american national standards institute common space means any land area and accompanying air space designated and improved as an area to accommodate specified public or community uses or activities common structure means any fabricated structure or facility designed designated and for use in accommodating specified public or community uses activities or equipment grade means surface of the ground or a structure either in its existing degree of inclination or as modified by development and construction mobile home means a manufactured home as defined in sc t meaning a structure transportable in one or more sections which in the traveling mode is eight body feet or more in width or 40 body feet or more in length or when erected on site is 320 or more square feet and which is built on a permanent chassis and designed to be used as a dwelling with or without a permanent foundation when connected to the required utilities and all systems appliances accessories and furnishings sold with the home including among other things the plumbing heating air conditioning and electrical systems mobile home accessory structures means a detached or separate subordinate structure intended to serve mobile home users and located upon the same tract or lot as the mobile home it serves mobile home park means a unified planned development of two or more mobile home lots on a single tract of land under single ownership and control mobile homes are not permanently secured to a permanent foundation in mobile home parks mobile home subdivision means a unified planned development of two or more mobile home lots on a single tract of land where lots are offered for sale rather than retained under single ownership mobile homes are permanently secured to a permanent foundation in mobile home subdivisions nfpa means national fire protection association open space means land area that is free from manmade structures or equipment person  the term person has its customary dictionary meaning except that plural usages include the singular and singular usages include the plural site means the exact area of ground upon which something is located sites are within tracts of land structure means something that is constructed by man tract means a designated and delineated area of land   art 4 secs 3653626  reserved article ii  development plan review application the provisions of this article shall apply to all mobile homes mobile home parks and mobile home subdivisions throughout the city 1  art 5  1 mobile homes permitted outside of approved mobile home parks or subdivisions mobile homes outside of approved mobile home parks or subdivisions shall be permitted only for public school or public health purposes or for such other public purposes as may be approved by the planning commission and for the purpose of providing a residence for a watchman upon the premises of an industrial or commercial facility located within an industrial or commercial zoning district anyone wishing to locate a mobile home outside an approved mobile home park or subdivision in the city must secure written approval by the city planning commission that the proposed location and conditions of location will be in conformance with the regulations of this article prior to seeking approval the applicant must also have exhibited evidence to the commission that the county health officer has issued the applicant a permit pursuant to state law as a condition of approval the applicant must purchase a mobile home license from the county tax auditor location approval or disapproval recommended by the planning commission shall be rendered to the applicant no later than 60 days from the date of the submission of such application in writing to the planning commission the planning commission shall recommend approval or disapproval of the proposed location based upon the facts submitted by the applicant in consideration of the objectives and criteria of this article applications shall include the following data and information in writing with graphic descriptions as necessary 1 proposed location of mobile home and its address with name and address of applicant 2 statement of receipt and date of approval by the county health officer for power hookup pursuant to state law 3 legal description of the tract upon which the mobile home is proposed to be located also including a dimensions and topographic descriptions b setbacks from tract boundary lines to the mobile homes exterior walls c distances from the mobile homes exterior walls to any other structure on the same or adjacent tract d proposed tract improvements e proposed and existing access systems including location width and surface of roads walkways entrances and exits and offstreet parking provisions f description and condition of proposed method of sewage disposal water supply solid waste removal and electrical supply g description of proposed method of securing mobile home to the ground h description of the use of the land environmental conditions and land and water features in all directions from the tract for a minimum of 250 feet horizontally when the tract is less than two acres in size when the tract is two acres or more in size the description shall pertain to the tract itself and a general description of lands adjoining the tract in addition to reviewing applications based upon the objectives and criteria of this article the commission shall have the authority to seek the review and comment of other governmental and quasigovernmental organizations prior to making its recommendation 2  art 5  2 approval of mobile home parks and subdivisions a in order to either subdivide land as a unified planned residential development or subdivision for mobile homes or to construct a mobile home park on a tract of land under single ownership the person wishing to do so must first secure written approval by the city planning commission prior to receiving approval the applicant must also have exhibited evidence to the commission that the county health officer has granted a permit to the applicant b recommendations on location and design approved by the commission shall be rendered to the applicant no later than 60 days from the date of the submission of such application in writing to the commission the planning commission shall recommend approval or disapproval of the proposed location and development plan based upon facts submitted by the applicant and its consideration of the objectives and criteria of this article applications shall include a development plan with the following data and registered professional engineer or land surveyor and showing the following a proposed tract and site design andor subdivision of land if any by size number and location of lots including proposed density ratio and setback  side and rear lot requirements whether on leased or sold lots b total park area including dimensions and topography with existing and proposed grades at five foot contour intervals  scale  and north arrow c proposed tract improvements for serviceutility buildings recreation facilities or other community facilities and amenities  and provisions for ensuring continued maintenance and upkeep d location size and surface of proposed access and circulation systems including all roads walkways bikeways entrances and exits and community parking areas  and provisions to ensure their continued maintenance and upkeep e location size and condition of all utility lines and systems and easements thereto 4 location description and condition by capacities and type of treatment of proposed method of sewage disposal and water supply and provisions to ensure their continued maintenance and operation 5 proposed method of solid waste removal electrical supply and fire protection improvements and provisions to ensure their continued operation and maintenance 6 proposed park regulations and lease covenants or deed restrictions of particular importance to the city are home tiedown requirements 7 description and assessment of the existing use of land environmental conditions and land and water features for the entire tract of land proposed for development and a
